\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_POINTER}{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_POINTER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER~((\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})0x01)}

Indicator that the next value in the {\ttfamily extra} parameter to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_x_e_c_ga920a0845a7a1e6dca2af5e51b9a00ab6}{cu\+Launch\+Kernel} will be a pointer to a buffer containing all kernel parameters used for launching kernel {\ttfamily f}. This buffer needs to honor all alignment/padding requirements of the individual parameters. If \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf339c057cd94562ead93a192e11c17e9}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+SIZE} is not also specified in the {\ttfamily extra} array, then \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER} will have no effect. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf339c057cd94562ead93a192e11c17e9}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf339c057cd94562ead93a192e11c17e9} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_SIZE@{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_SIZE}}
\index{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_SIZE@{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_SIZE}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_SIZE}{CU\_LAUNCH\_PARAM\_BUFFER\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+SIZE~((\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{void}}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})0x02)}

Indicator that the next value in the {\ttfamily extra} parameter to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_x_e_c_ga920a0845a7a1e6dca2af5e51b9a00ab6}{cu\+Launch\+Kernel} will be a pointer to a size\+\_\+t which contains the size of the buffer specified with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER}. It is required that \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga36d10d0b40c51372877578a2cffd6acd}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+POINTER} also be specified in the {\ttfamily extra} array if the value associated with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf339c057cd94562ead93a192e11c17e9}{CU\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+BUFFER\+\_\+\+SIZE} is not zero. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad5c11cff5adfa5a69d66829399653532}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad5c11cff5adfa5a69d66829399653532}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP~0x02}

\index{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_PORTABLE@{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_PORTABLE}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_PORTABLE}{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_PORTABLE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+PORTABLE~0x01}

If set, host memory is portable between CUDA contexts. Flag for \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc()} \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga7361580951deecace15352c97a210038}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga7361580951deecace15352c97a210038} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_WRITECOMBINED@{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_WRITECOMBINED}}
\index{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_WRITECOMBINED@{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_WRITECOMBINED}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_WRITECOMBINED}{CU\_MEMHOSTALLOC\_WRITECOMBINED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTALLOC\+\_\+\+WRITECOMBINED~0x04}

If set, host memory is allocated as write-\/combined -\/ fast to write, faster to DMA, slow to read except via SSE4 streaming load instruction (MOVNTDQA). Flag for \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_gada6927828b81f5415eb0a7cb0134e522}{cu\+Mem\+Host\+Alloc()} \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf1fc8645f0ab5481e7be96c80f6bfa50}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf1fc8645f0ab5481e7be96c80f6bfa50} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_DEVICEMAP@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_DEVICEMAP}}
\index{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_DEVICEMAP@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_DEVICEMAP}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_DEVICEMAP}{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_DEVICEMAP}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+DEVICEMAP~0x02}

If set, host memory is mapped into CUDA address space and cu\+Mem\+Host\+Get\+Device\+Pointer() may be called on the host pointer. Flag for cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register() \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6a86cf1a826f8da5b01f1b5cd8da2bde}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga6a86cf1a826f8da5b01f1b5cd8da2bde} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_IOMEMORY@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_IOMEMORY}}
\index{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_IOMEMORY@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_IOMEMORY}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_IOMEMORY}{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_IOMEMORY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+IOMEMORY~0x04}

If set, the passed memory pointer is treated as pointing to some memory-\/mapped I/O space, e.\+g. belonging to a third-\/party PCIe device. On Windows the flag is a no-\/op. On Linux that memory is marked as non cache-\/coherent for the GPU and is expected to be physically contiguous. It may return \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaae23d0197c490ec332a43e55b167968a3}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+PERMITTED} if run as an unprivileged user, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa54756ae7ade0dfd09faeccb513dd831b}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED} on older Linux kernel versions. On all other platforms, it is not supported and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa54756ae7ade0dfd09faeccb513dd831b}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED} is returned. Flag for cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register() \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga4f20a39f0a7bddc8ce7d644327a2e7da}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga4f20a39f0a7bddc8ce7d644327a2e7da} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_PORTABLE@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_PORTABLE}}
\index{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_PORTABLE@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_PORTABLE}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_PORTABLE}{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_PORTABLE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+PORTABLE~0x01}

If set, host memory is portable between CUDA contexts. Flag for cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register() \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad870d49634958b801f5c02a6ba459a1a}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad870d49634958b801f5c02a6ba459a1a} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_READ\_ONLY@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_READ\_ONLY}}
\index{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_READ\_ONLY@{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_READ\_ONLY}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_READ\_ONLY}{CU\_MEMHOSTREGISTER\_READ\_ONLY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+MEMHOSTREGISTER\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ONLY~0x08}

If set, the passed memory pointer is treated as pointing to memory that is considered read-\/only by the device. On platforms without \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa52c58d6fd1d3a72673cce199ab30cd40}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+PAGEABLE\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+USES\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+PAGE\+\_\+\+TABLES}, this flag is required in order to register memory mapped to the CPU as read-\/only. Support for the use of this flag can be queried from the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa3a3a9091a7991536d507dd5eff146d2b}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ONLY\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+REGISTER\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED}. Using this flag with a current context associated with a device that does not have this attribute set will cause cu\+Mem\+Host\+Register to error with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa54756ae7ade0dfd09faeccb513dd831b}{CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED}. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga3e9be6955a6a5c311ad5ea2debdd6613}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga3e9be6955a6a5c311ad5ea2debdd6613} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_PARAM\_TR\_DEFAULT@{CU\_PARAM\_TR\_DEFAULT}}
\index{CU\_PARAM\_TR\_DEFAULT@{CU\_PARAM\_TR\_DEFAULT}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CU\_PARAM\_TR\_DEFAULT}{CU\_PARAM\_TR\_DEFAULT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+PARAM\+\_\+\+TR\+\_\+\+DEFAULT~-\/1}

For texture references loaded into the module, use default texunit from texture reference. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaa53e8210837f039dd6434a3a4c3324aa}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaa53e8210837f039dd6434a3a4c3324aa}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CU\+\_\+\+TRSA\+\_\+\+OVERRIDE\+\_\+\+FORMAT~0x01}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CUDA\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+SEMAPHORE\+\_\+\+SIGNAL\+\_\+\+SKIP\+\_\+\+NVSCIBUF\+\_\+\+MEMSYNC~0x01}

When the {\ttfamily flags} parameter of CUDA\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+SEMAPHORE\+\_\+\+SIGNAL\+\_\+\+PARAMS contains this flag, it indicates that signaling an external semaphore object should skip performing appropriate memory synchronization operations over all the external memory objects that are imported as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggafe2bee7f51d487e11f460752088812a8aadf93206205d155aed8228f4a118d6ee}{CU\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+HANDLE\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+NVSCIBUF}, which otherwise are performed by default to ensure data coherency with other importers of the same Nv\+Sci\+Buf memory objects. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf07a1d15f2696b915c068c892e6f1a35}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf07a1d15f2696b915c068c892e6f1a35}

\index{CUDA\_EXTERNAL\_SEMAPHORE\_WAIT\_SKIP\_NVSCIBUF\_MEMSYNC@{CUDA\_EXTERNAL\_SEMAPHORE\_WAIT\_SKIP\_NVSCIBUF\_MEMSYNC}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CUDA\_EXTERNAL\_SEMAPHORE\_WAIT\_SKIP\_NVSCIBUF\_MEMSYNC}{CUDA\_EXTERNAL\_SEMAPHORE\_WAIT\_SKIP\_NVSCIBUF\_MEMSYNC}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{define}} CUDA\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+SEMAPHORE\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+SKIP\+\_\+\+NVSCIBUF\+\_\+\+MEMSYNC~0x02}

When the {\ttfamily flags} parameter of CUDA\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+SEMAPHORE\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+PARAMS contains this flag, it indicates that waiting on an external semaphore object should skip performing appropriate memory synchronization operations over all the external memory objects that are imported as \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggafe2bee7f51d487e11f460752088812a8aadf93206205d155aed8228f4a118d6ee}{CU\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+HANDLE\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+NVSCIBUF}, which otherwise are performed by default to ensure data coherency with other importers of the same Nv\+Sci\+Buf memory objects. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga8709811eaf5a7849ad235aae65471a06}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga8709811eaf5a7849ad235aae65471a06}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CUaccessPolicyWindow\_v1}{CUaccessPolicyWindow\_v1}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{typedef}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{struct}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_c_uaccess_policy_window__st}{CUaccess\+Policy\+Window\+\_\+st}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga2df38b7f12843446affce2508fe3fe21}{CUaccess\+Policy\+Window\+\_\+v1}}}

Specifies an access policy for a window, a contiguous extent of memory beginning at base\+\_\+ptr and ending at base\+\_\+ptr + num\+\_\+bytes. num\+\_\+bytes is limited by CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+ACCESS\+\_\+\+POLICY\+\_\+\+WINDOW\+\_\+\+SIZE. Partition into many segments and assign segments such that\+: sum of "{}hit segments"{} / window == approx. ratio. sum of "{}miss segments"{} / window == approx 1-\/ratio. Segments and ratio specifications are fitted to the capabilities of the architecture. Accesses in a hit segment apply the hit\+Prop access policy. Accesses in a miss segment apply the miss\+Prop access policy. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae197d9271fd7a0d8cd6ceca5c3b09001}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gae197d9271fd7a0d8cd6ceca5c3b09001}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CUeglResourceLocationFlags}{CUeglResourceLocationFlags}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{typedef}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35a}{CUegl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags\+\_\+enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaa9c90614957a62578d68c823f189e93e}{CUegl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags}}}

Resource location flags-\/ sysmem or vidmem

For CUDA context on i\+GPU, since video and system memory are equivalent -\/ these flags will not have an effect on the execution.

For CUDA context on d\+GPU, applications can use the flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaa9c90614957a62578d68c823f189e93e}{CUegl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags} to give a hint about the desired location.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa0033e7197256284919d4dd8f8a45482a}{CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+RESOURCE\+\_\+\+LOCATION\+\_\+\+SYSMEM} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the system memory to be accessed by CUDA.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa115dedc3b0a393b00d2c38d996daeedc}{CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+RESOURCE\+\_\+\+LOCATION\+\_\+\+VIDMEM} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the dedicated video memory to be accessed by CUDA.

There may be an additional latency due to new allocation and data migration, if the frame is produced on a different memory. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga60c595264697050bc2bb8e00cf5f86e7}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga60c595264697050bc2bb8e00cf5f86e7}

CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+CONTEXT&This most frequently indicates that there is no context bound to the current thread. This can also be returned if the context passed to an API call is not a valid handle (such as a context that has had cu\+Ctx\+Destroy() invoked on it). This can also be returned if a user mixes different API versions (i.\+e. 3010 context with 3020 API calls). See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___c_t_x_gaba93fa1c4a4f3da76d87704716a3d3c0}{cu\+Ctx\+Get\+Api\+Version()} for more details. \\

CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+CONTEXT\+\_\+\+ALREADY\+\_\+\+CURRENT&This indicated that the context being supplied as a parameter to the API call was already the active context. \begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}

CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+RESOURCES&This indicates that a launch did not occur because it did not have appropriate resources. This error usually indicates that the user has attempted to pass too many arguments to the device kernel, or the kernel launch specifies too many threads for the kernel\textquotesingle{}s register count. Passing arguments of the wrong size (i.\+e. a 64-\/bit pointer when a 32-\/bit int is expected) is equivalent to passing too many arguments and can also result in this error. \\

CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+PC&While executing a kernel, the device program counter wrapped its address space. This leaves the process in an inconsistent state and any further CUDA work will return the same error. To continue using CUDA, the process must be terminated and relaunched. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CUDA\_ERROR\_LAUNCH\_FAILED@{CUDA\_ERROR\_LAUNCH\_FAILED}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CUDA\_ERROR\_LAUNCH\_FAILED@{CUDA\_ERROR\_LAUNCH\_FAILED}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa4f270bc1011b152febc8154b2b1e1b8d}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaa4f270bc1011b152febc8154b2b1e1b8d} 
CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+FAILED&An exception occurred on the device while executing a kernel. Common causes include dereferencing an invalid device pointer and accessing out of bounds shared memory. Less common cases can be system specific -\/ more information about these cases can be found in the system specific user guide. This leaves the process in an inconsistent state and any further CUDA work will return the same error. To continue using CUDA, the process must be terminated and relaunched. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CUDA\_ERROR\_COOPERATIVE\_LAUNCH\_TOO\_LARGE@{CUDA\_ERROR\_COOPERATIVE\_LAUNCH\_TOO\_LARGE}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CUDA\_ERROR\_COOPERATIVE\_LAUNCH\_TOO\_LARGE@{CUDA\_ERROR\_COOPERATIVE\_LAUNCH\_TOO\_LARGE}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaad26f67e0acc1563f87ddb94c638478cd}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaad26f67e0acc1563f87ddb94c638478cd} 
CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+COOPERATIVE\+\_\+\+LAUNCH\+\_\+\+TOO\+\_\+\+LARGE&This error indicates that the number of blocks launched per grid for a kernel that was launched via either \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_x_e_c_gaeb5259b5a28ee4379d905bee4827a767}{cu\+Launch\+Cooperative\+Kernel} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_x_e_c_ga79550cda1439bb78af5094ddabe8eac0}{cu\+Launch\+Cooperative\+Kernel\+Multi\+Device} exceeds the maximum number of blocks as allowed by \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___o_c_c_u_p_a_n_c_y_gae81e36f2257cd84ef167e39ac98a4bc8}{cu\+Occupancy\+Max\+Active\+Blocks\+Per\+Multiprocessor} or \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___o_c_c_u_p_a_n_c_y_ga30ea39b7e266a235bfa08b593b1063b7}{cu\+Occupancy\+Max\+Active\+Blocks\+Per\+Multiprocessor\+With\+Flags} times the number of multiprocessors as specified by the device attribute \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aab92d0a38a94a3f61d4c53e00114afcaa}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MULTIPROCESSOR\+\_\+\+COUNT}. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CUDA\_ERROR\_EXTERNAL\_DEVICE@{CUDA\_ERROR\_EXTERNAL\_DEVICE}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CUDA\_ERROR\_EXTERNAL\_DEVICE@{CUDA\_ERROR\_EXTERNAL\_DEVICE}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaceb154e2a824d8397aee018dea64d7ad}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga0cdead942fd5028d157641eef6bdeeaaaceb154e2a824d8397aee018dea64d7ad} 
CUDA\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+EXTERNAL\+\_\+\+DEVICE&This indicates that an async error has occurred in a device outside of CUDA. If CUDA was waiting for an external device\textquotesingle{}s signal before consuming shared data, the external device signaled an error indicating that the data is not valid for consumption. This leaves the process in an inconsistent state and any further CUDA work will return the same error. To continue using CUDA, the process must be terminated and relaunched. \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga8852082a4157dd2ea18d91ea9d0b3502}{CUegl\+Color\+Format\+\_\+enum}}}

CUDA EGL Color Format -\/ The different planar and multiplanar formats currently supported for CUDA\+\_\+\+EGL interops. Three channel formats are currently not supported for \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggaf9e66bcc793cb26cf62399e7e8ed782aac02019e2bb4a56d31db30925d567d101}{CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+FRAME\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+ARRAY} \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_PLANAR@{CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_PLANAR}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_PLANAR@{CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_PLANAR}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga8852082a4157dd2ea18d91ea9d0b3502a295e95d7455d1da1d7c21ff7e6644de4}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga8852082a4157dd2ea18d91ea9d0b3502a295e95d7455d1da1d7c21ff7e6644de4} 
CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+COLOR\+\_\+\+FORMAT\+\_\+\+YUV420\+\_\+\+PLANAR&Y, U, V in three surfaces, each in a separate surface, U/V width = 1/2 Y width, U/V height = 1/2 Y height. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_SEMIPLANAR@{CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_SEMIPLANAR}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_SEMIPLANAR@{CU\_EGL\_COLOR\_FORMAT\_YUV420\_SEMIPLANAR}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga8852082a4157dd2ea18d91ea9d0b3502a2e97422d70b28f8528310af95260ef9e}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga8852082a4157dd2ea18d91ea9d0b3502a2e97422d70b28f8528310af95260ef9e}

\index{CUeglResourceLocationFlags\_enum@{CUeglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CUeglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}{CUeglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35a}{CUegl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags\+\_\+enum}}}

Resource location flags-\/ sysmem or vidmem

For CUDA context on i\+GPU, since video and system memory are equivalent -\/ these flags will not have an effect on the execution.

For CUDA context on d\+GPU, applications can use the flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaa9c90614957a62578d68c823f189e93e}{CUegl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags} to give a hint about the desired location.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa0033e7197256284919d4dd8f8a45482a}{CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+RESOURCE\+\_\+\+LOCATION\+\_\+\+SYSMEM} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the system memory to be accessed by CUDA.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa115dedc3b0a393b00d2c38d996daeedc}{CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+RESOURCE\+\_\+\+LOCATION\+\_\+\+VIDMEM} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the dedicated video memory to be accessed by CUDA.

There may be an additional latency due to new allocation and data migration, if the frame is produced on a different memory. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_SYSMEM@{CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_SYSMEM}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_SYSMEM@{CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_SYSMEM}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa0033e7197256284919d4dd8f8a45482a}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa0033e7197256284919d4dd8f8a45482a} 
CU\+\_\+\+EGL\+\_\+\+RESOURCE\+\_\+\+LOCATION\+\_\+\+SYSMEM&Resource location sysmem \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_VIDMEM@{CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_VIDMEM}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_VIDMEM@{CU\_EGL\_RESOURCE\_LOCATION\_VIDMEM}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa115dedc3b0a393b00d2c38d996daeedc}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3c8fee650dc5b3fbd433dcebec76b35aa115dedc3b0a393b00d2c38d996daeedc}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36}{CUfunction\+\_\+attribute\+\_\+enum}}}

Function properties \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36aa244b9a52d7426e6684acebf4c9e24b8}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36aa244b9a52d7426e6684acebf4c9e24b8} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+THREADS\+\_\+\+PER\+\_\+\+BLOCK&The maximum number of threads per block, beyond which a launch of the function would fail. This number depends on both the function and the device on which the function is currently loaded. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a15651a634781263c9d4ee6070a3991f4}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a15651a634781263c9d4ee6070a3991f4} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+SHARED\+\_\+\+SIZE\+\_\+\+BYTES&The size in bytes of statically-\/allocated shared memory required by this function. This does not include dynamically-\/allocated shared memory requested by the user at runtime. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CONST\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CONST\_SIZE\_BYTES}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CONST\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CONST\_SIZE\_BYTES}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a4a255dc4e2b8542e84c9431c1953a952}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a4a255dc4e2b8542e84c9431c1953a952} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CONST\+\_\+\+SIZE\+\_\+\+BYTES&The size in bytes of user-\/allocated constant memory required by this function. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_LOCAL\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_LOCAL\_SIZE\_BYTES}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_LOCAL\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_LOCAL\_SIZE\_BYTES}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a0318e60c17eb22c70ffb59f610c504dd}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a0318e60c17eb22c70ffb59f610c504dd} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+LOCAL\+\_\+\+SIZE\+\_\+\+BYTES&The size in bytes of local memory used by each thread of this function. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_NUM\_REGS@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_NUM\_REGS}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_NUM\_REGS@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_NUM\_REGS}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a217730c04b1edbc80bb1772c1d6a7752}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a217730c04b1edbc80bb1772c1d6a7752} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+NUM\+\_\+\+REGS&The number of registers used by each thread of this function. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PTX\_VERSION@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PTX\_VERSION}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PTX\_VERSION@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PTX\_VERSION}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36acbd28200668ad2de39035446a89bf930}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36acbd28200668ad2de39035446a89bf930} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+PTX\+\_\+\+VERSION&The PTX virtual architecture version for which the function was compiled. This value is the major PTX version \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 10 + the minor PTX version, so a PTX version 1.\+3 function would return the value 13. Note that this may return the undefined value of 0 for cubins compiled prior to CUDA 3.\+0. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_BINARY\_VERSION@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_BINARY\_VERSION}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_BINARY\_VERSION@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_BINARY\_VERSION}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36ac4f70f5d16889d0b75c3bf7a303eb437}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36ac4f70f5d16889d0b75c3bf7a303eb437} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+BINARY\+\_\+\+VERSION&The binary architecture version for which the function was compiled. This value is the major binary version \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 10 + the minor binary version, so a binary version 1.\+3 function would return the value 13. Note that this will return a value of 10 for legacy cubins that do not have a properly-\/encoded binary architecture version. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CACHE\_MODE\_CA@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CACHE\_MODE\_CA}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CACHE\_MODE\_CA@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_CACHE\_MODE\_CA}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a9f9c76a76921445e8bdb92d74e6a3271}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a9f9c76a76921445e8bdb92d74e6a3271} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CACHE\+\_\+\+MODE\+\_\+\+CA&The attribute to indicate whether the function has been compiled with user specified option "{}-\/\+Xptxas -\/-\/dlcm=ca"{} set . \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_DYNAMIC\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_DYNAMIC\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_DYNAMIC\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_MAX\_DYNAMIC\_SHARED\_SIZE\_BYTES}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a75b33d145e83462ef7292575015be03e}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36a75b33d145e83462ef7292575015be03e} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+DYNAMIC\+\_\+\+SHARED\+\_\+\+SIZE\+\_\+\+BYTES&The maximum size in bytes of dynamically-\/allocated shared memory that can be used by this function. If the user-\/specified dynamic shared memory size is larger than this value, the launch will fail. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_x_e_c_ga68d6d7c16f1544866530ff0f3be72f17}{cu\+Func\+Set\+Attribute} \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PREFERRED\_SHARED\_MEMORY\_CARVEOUT@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PREFERRED\_SHARED\_MEMORY\_CARVEOUT}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PREFERRED\_SHARED\_MEMORY\_CARVEOUT@{CU\_FUNC\_ATTRIBUTE\_PREFERRED\_SHARED\_MEMORY\_CARVEOUT}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36ac75f6fd470b848653f026b8c82c10ae3}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggab67889469b7e66d222f5dbe69bbfdf36ac75f6fd470b848653f026b8c82c10ae3} 
CU\+\_\+\+FUNC\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+PREFERRED\+\_\+\+SHARED\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+CARVEOUT&On devices where the L1 cache and shared memory use the same hardware resources, this sets the shared memory carveout preference, in percent of the total shared memory. Refer to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aa06a33c18889f6fc907412451c95154ed}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+SHARED\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+PER\+\_\+\+MULTIPROCESSOR}. This is only a hint, and the driver can choose a different ratio if required to execute the function. See \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___e_x_e_c_ga68d6d7c16f1544866530ff0f3be72f17}{cu\+Func\+Set\+Attribute} \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_JIT\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK@{CU\_JIT\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_JIT\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK@{CU\_JIT\_THREADS\_PER\_BLOCK}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggafaa9995214a4f3341f48c5830cea0d8aae2d4d9ff4fbd21f21039f182616ba1fc}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggafaa9995214a4f3341f48c5830cea0d8aae2d4d9ff4fbd21f21039f182616ba1fc} 
CU\+\_\+\+JIT\+\_\+\+THREADS\+\_\+\+PER\+\_\+\+BLOCK&IN\+: Specifies minimum number of threads per block to target compilation for~\newline
OUT\+: Returns the number of threads the compiler actually targeted. This restricts the resource utilization fo the compiler (e.\+g. max registers) such that a block with the given number of threads should be able to launch based on register limitations. Note, this option does not currently take into account any other resource limitations, such as shared memory utilization.~\newline
Cannot be combined with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ggafaa9995214a4f3341f48c5830cea0d8aa3bf12ddeaa2a9d64db4d20de537cd596}{CU\+\_\+\+JIT\+\_\+\+TARGET}.~\newline
Option type\+: unsigned int~\newline
Applies to\+: compiler only \\

CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+REUSE\+\_\+\+FOLLOW\+\_\+\+EVENT\+\_\+\+DEPENDENCIES&(value type = int) Allow cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Async to use memory asynchronously freed in another streams as long as a stream ordering dependency of the allocating stream on the free action exists. Cuda events and null stream interactions can create the required stream ordered dependencies. (default enabled) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_OPPORTUNISTIC@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_OPPORTUNISTIC}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_OPPORTUNISTIC@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_OPPORTUNISTIC}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5ad1016ed326b53c1eb06e8da5d40359cb}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5ad1016ed326b53c1eb06e8da5d40359cb} 
CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+REUSE\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+OPPORTUNISTIC&(value type = int) Allow reuse of already completed frees when there is no dependency between the free and allocation. (default enabled) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_INTERNAL\_DEPENDENCIES@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_INTERNAL\_DEPENDENCIES}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_INTERNAL\_DEPENDENCIES@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_REUSE\_ALLOW\_INTERNAL\_DEPENDENCIES}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a3b7973c1b89f3a05f26702ade1124e9f}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a3b7973c1b89f3a05f26702ade1124e9f} 
CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+REUSE\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+INTERNAL\+\_\+\+DEPENDENCIES&(value type = int) Allow cu\+Mem\+Alloc\+Async to insert new stream dependencies in order to establish the stream ordering required to reuse a piece of memory released by cu\+Free\+Async (default enabled). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RELEASE\_THRESHOLD@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RELEASE\_THRESHOLD}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RELEASE\_THRESHOLD@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RELEASE\_THRESHOLD}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a50fa2c731b01422ffbeb8c16ce0ba9a8}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a50fa2c731b01422ffbeb8c16ce0ba9a8} 
CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+RELEASE\+\_\+\+THRESHOLD&(value type = cuuint64\+\_\+t) Amount of reserved memory in bytes to hold onto before trying to release memory back to the OS. When more than the release threshold bytes of memory are held by the memory pool, the allocator will try to release memory back to the OS on the next call to stream, event or context synchronize. (default 0) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_CURRENT@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_CURRENT}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_CURRENT@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_CURRENT}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5aecd4938eb06ce224e04d4c56fea476c6}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5aecd4938eb06ce224e04d4c56fea476c6} 
CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+RESERVED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+CURRENT&(value type = cuuint64\+\_\+t) Amount of backing memory currently allocated for the mempool. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_HIGH@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_HIGH}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_HIGH@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_RESERVED\_MEM\_HIGH}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a5ccb2736772fd27a735f15905118cbf6}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a5ccb2736772fd27a735f15905118cbf6} 
CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+RESERVED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+HIGH&(value type = cuuint64\+\_\+t) High watermark of backing memory allocated for the mempool since the last time it was reset. High watermark can only be reset to zero. \\

CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+USED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+CURRENT&(value type = cuuint64\+\_\+t) Amount of memory from the pool that is currently in use by the application. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_USED\_MEM\_HIGH@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_USED\_MEM\_HIGH}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_USED\_MEM\_HIGH@{CU\_MEMPOOL\_ATTR\_USED\_MEM\_HIGH}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a27fd3cf6d5a152572e55e9736da6987b}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga62d6f30fb3d1f10083991ffeb8ed7ef5a27fd3cf6d5a152572e55e9736da6987b} 
CU\+\_\+\+MEMPOOL\+\_\+\+ATTR\+\_\+\+USED\+\_\+\+MEM\+\_\+\+HIGH&(value type = cuuint64\+\_\+t) High watermark of the amount of memory from the pool that was in use by the application since the last time it was reset. High watermark can only be reset to zero. \\

Support for this operation can be queried with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___d_e_v_i_c_e_ga5a73f28b53203cd6097fc48d97ca4ead}{cu\+Device\+Get\+Attribute()} and \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga3b9f561d2a42733dde99b2cedcaa413aabe06f9c31c264e0b29be6cc6330b5047}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CAN\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+STREAM\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+VALUE\+\_\+\+NOR}. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_STREAM\_WAIT\_VALUE\_FLUSH@{CU\_STREAM\_WAIT\_VALUE\_FLUSH}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_STREAM\_WAIT\_VALUE\_FLUSH@{CU\_STREAM\_WAIT\_VALUE\_FLUSH}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga5ba489253eb905a983228a810c1f3360a5dd93e7173619c943fae495568f4d771}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga5ba489253eb905a983228a810c1f3360a5dd93e7173619c943fae495568f4d771} 
CU\+\_\+\+STREAM\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+VALUE\+\_\+\+FLUSH&Follow the wait operation with a flush of outstanding remote writes. This means that, if a remote write operation is guaranteed to have reached the device before the wait can be satisfied, that write is guaranteed to be visible to downstream device work. The device is permitted to reorder remote writes internally. For example, this flag would be required if two remote writes arrive in a defined order, the wait is satisfied by the second write, and downstream work needs to observe the first write. Support for this operation is restricted to selected platforms and can be queried with \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+ATTRIBUTE\+\_\+\+CAN\+\_\+\+USE\+\_\+\+WAIT\+\_\+\+VALUE\+\_\+\+FLUSH}. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{CU\_STREAM\_WRITE\_VALUE\_NO\_MEMORY\_BARRIER@{CU\_STREAM\_WRITE\_VALUE\_NO\_MEMORY\_BARRIER}!Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}}\index{Data types used by CUDA driver@{Data types used by CUDA driver}!CU\_STREAM\_WRITE\_VALUE\_NO\_MEMORY\_BARRIER@{CU\_STREAM\_WRITE\_VALUE\_NO\_MEMORY\_BARRIER}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga943b07fd5ca680062cd270aa714b1c32a52598852c1a097794bc7d08576f94995}\label{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gga943b07fd5ca680062cd270aa714b1c32a52598852c1a097794bc7d08576f94995} 
CU\+\_\+\+STREAM\+\_\+\+WRITE\+\_\+\+VALUE\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+BARRIER&Permits the write to be reordered with writes which were issued before it, as a performance optimization. Normally, \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a___m_e_m_o_p_ga3f0dab1d1fe1f885ae4128db7eddbb26}{cu\+Stream\+Write\+Value32} will provide a memory fence before the write, which has similar semantics to \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{\+\_\+\+\_\+threadfence\+\_\+system()} but is scoped to the stream rather than a CUDA thread. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}
